<a name="842"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_ajax_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">请求(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; cursor: pointer; outline: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(43, 119, 197); font-family: Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, &quot;\\5FAE软雅黑&quot;, &quot;\\5B8B体&quot;, &quot;Malgun Gothic&quot;, Meiryo, sans-serif; font-style: italic; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 14px;">request</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">)--处理-- 响应(</span><span style="letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Arial, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, &quot;\\5FAE软雅黑&quot;, &quot;\\5B8B体&quot;, &quot;Malgun Gothic&quot;, Meiryo, sans-serif; font-variant: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 10.5px;">respond</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">xhr 请求服务器上的数据</span></div><div>
</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">get 请求 拿资源</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">post 请求 发送资源</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">ajax基于jQ</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">异步请求</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">$.get() 拿数据   [data]格式为对象{id:1}</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [27].png)</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">$.post(url,[data],[callback]) 发数据</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">$.ajax()  拿数据和发数据</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [28].png)</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">error:function(){</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">服务器连接失败触发</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">};</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">timeout:2000,  设置访问时间不能超过2000毫秒</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">complete:function(){'无论成功还是失败都会触发'} </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">headers: {'请求的头部,携带的参数'}</span></div><div>
</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">jq的ajax请求 后台不做任何要求情况下,我们可以传字符串也可以传对象</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">实际开发传数据,都要转成对象格</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">式</span></div><div>
</div><div>
</div><div>每次发请求前都能拦截到</div><div>![](前端_files/Image [29].png)</div><div>
</div></span>
</div>

<a name="850"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_ajax_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div><div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">form 表单的属性</span></font></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">action:向何处发送表单数据</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">target:_blank:新的标签  _self:自身跳转</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">method: get(默认)和post</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">enctype:  编码格式   涉及文件上传要修改</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">表单缺点:同步提交  跳转 页面之前数据和状态丢失</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">reset():清空表单  原生的方法</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        </span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">通过ajax 提交表单数据</span></font></div>

1.  <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">获取表单(form)</span></div>
2.  <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">监听表单(form)提交事件 submit事件</span></div>
3.  <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">阻止表单默认行为</span><span style="letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;, Consolas, Courier, monospace; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">event.preventDefault()</span></div>
4.  <div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;;">serialize() 获取所有表单元素,每个元素必须有name属性 || </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;;">serializeArray获取数组格式的数据</span></font></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
    </font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">模板引擎   template('模板id',需要渲染的数据)</span></font></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">1导入js文件</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">2定义渲染的数据  只能是对象格式</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">3定义模板 &lt;script type=&quot;text/html&quot; id=&quot;a&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;</span></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">!!!type  和  id属性必须写 </span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">  标准语法{{}}数据占位符(参考对象的结构,属性名自动匹配值)</span></div>*   <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">4调用template()函数</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">5渲染到页面</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold;">正则exec()方法 :  匹配到返回一个数组,匹配不到返回null1</span></span></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold;">模板引擎核心原理,利用字符串的replace()方法配合正则表达式和while循环实现字符串的多次替换</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">   </span></div><div>
  </div></span>
  </div>

<a name="860"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_ajax_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div>

- <div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">xhr发起GET请求</span></font></div><div>            ![](前端_files/Image [31].png)</div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">xhr发起POST请求</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">        ![](前端_files/Image [32].png)</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
  </span></span></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">get 查询的本质</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">  参数以</span> <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);font-size: 14pt;-evernote-highlight:true;">查询字符串形式(url地址?后面的数据)</span> <span style="font-size: 14pt;">拼接到url地址后面</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
  </font></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">url 编码 </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">encodeURI</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">url 解码</span> <span style="font-size: 14pt;">decodeURI</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
  </font></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">xml 数据的载体 (不常用)</span></div>
- <div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">json 主流数据格式   本质是字符串</span></font></div><div>            ![](前端_files/Image [33].png)</div><div>
  </div>

- <div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">序列化  对象转字符串   JSON.stringify()</span></font></div>
- <div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">反序列化   字符串转对象  JSON.parse()</span></font></div><div>
  </div><div>
  </div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">获取上传的文件.files</span></font>  <span style="font-size: 12pt;">原生的方法 </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">文件上传表单的方法  得到</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">文件上传的列表 </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">是一个伪数组, 第0项是上传的数据</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [34].png)</div><div>
  </div><div>![](前端_files/Image [35].png)</div><div>![](前端_files/Image [36].png)</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
  </font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">jq上传文件</span></font></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; line-height: 27px;">log</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; line-height: 27px;">)</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    }</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">     })</span></div><div>
  </div></div><div>
  </div><div>![](前端_files/Image [37].png)</div><div>
  </div><div>
  </div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">jq中实现 文件上传显示进度</span></font></div><div>
  </div><div>![](前端_files/Image [38].png)</div><div>
  </div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">jq中监听Ajax请求被发起和停止 必须给 </span>**<span style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165); font-weight: bold; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;-evernote-highlight:true;">$</span><span style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165); font-weight: bold; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;-evernote-highlight:true;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165); font-weight: bold; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;-evernote-highlight:true;">'document'</span>**<span style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"><span style="font-size: 20px; background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px; font-weight: bold;-evernote-highlight:true;">)</span> 添加</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">ajaxStart</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">ajaxStop</span></div><div>
  </div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">在当前Ajax 请求之前</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">beforeSend:function(){}</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [39].png)</div><div>
  </div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">axios</span></font></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [40].png)</div><div>
  </div><div>![](前端_files/Image [41].png)</div><div>

</div></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align: middle; background-color: rgb(234, 234, 234); border: 1px solid rgb(187, 187, 187); width: 202px; padding: 8px;"><div>查看提交历史</div></td><td style="width: 654px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 按时间先后顺序列出所有的提交历史，最近的提交在最上面</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git log</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 只展示最新的两条提交历史，数字可以按需进行填写</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git log -2</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 在一行上展示最近两条提交历史的信息</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git log -2 --pretty=oneline</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 在一行上展示最近两条提交历史信息，并自定义输出的格式</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># &amp;h 提交的简写哈希值  %an 作者名字  %ar 作者修订日志  %s 提交说明</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git log -2 --pretty=format:&quot;%h | %an | %ar | %s&quot;</span></div></td><td style="width: 317px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align: middle; background-color: rgb(234, 234, 234); border: 1px solid rgb(187, 187, 187); width: 202px; padding: 8px;"><div>回退到历史版本</div></td><td style="width: 654px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 在一行上展示所有的提交历史</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git log --pretty=oneline</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 使用 git reset --hard 命令，根据指定的提交 ID 回退到指定版本</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git reset --hard &lt;CommitID&gt;</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 在旧版本中使用 git reflog --pretty=oneline 命令，查看命令操作的历史</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git reflog --pretty=onelone</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(251, 205, 95); font-weight: bold;"># 再次根据最新的提交 ID，跳转到最新的版本</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git reset --hard &lt;CommitID&gt;</span></div></td><td style="width: 317px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align: middle; background-color: rgb(234, 234, 234); border: 1px solid rgb(187, 187, 187); width: 202px; padding: 8px;"><div>

<a name="916"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_git_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div><div>开源许可协议   GPL强制开源   MIT</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">远程仓库的使用</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">新建远程仓库 </span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">两种访问方式</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">HTTPS: 不用配置,每次访问都需要输入密码  </span></font>![](前端_files/Image [51].png)                  </div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">git push    提交更新到远程仓库</span></div><div>
</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">SSH 需要进行配置 ,配置成功后不需要重复的输入github的账号和密码</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">私钥文件放在本地电脑中,公钥文件在github上面配置</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">生成SSH key</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">① 打开 Git Bash</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">② 粘贴如下的命令，并将 your_email@example.com 替换为注册 Github 账号时填写的邮箱：</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">* ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096 -C &quot;your_email@example.com&quot;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">③ 连续敲击 3 次回车，即可在 C:\Users\用户名文件夹\.ssh 目录中生成 id_rsa 和 id_rsa.pub 两个文件</font></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0.8em 0px; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold;">配置SHH key</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">① 使用记事本打开 id_rsa.pub 文件，复制里面的文本内容</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">② 在浏览器中登录 Github，点击头像 -&gt; Settings -&gt; SSH and GPG Keys -&gt; New SSH key</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">③ 将 id_rsa.pub 文件中的内容，粘贴到 Key 对应的文本框中</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">④ 在 Title 文本框中任意填写一个名称，来标识这个 Key 从何而来</font></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0.8em 0px; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">![](前端_files/Image [52].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">将远程仓库克隆到本地  </span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git clone 远程仓库的地址</font></div></div><div style="min-height: 9pt; text-align: left;">
</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">Git分支</span></font></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [53].png)</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">查看分支列表</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git branch</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">创建分支列表</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git branch 分支名称</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">切换分支类表</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git checkout 要切换到的分支列表</font></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">分支的快速创建和切换</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># -b 表示创建一个新分支</font></div><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># checkout 表示切换到刚才新建的分支上</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git checkout -b 分支名称  <font color="#DE5700">是创建分支和切换分支列表得简写</font></font></div></div><div>
</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">合并分支</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 1. 切换到 master 主分支</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git checkout master</font></div><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 2. 在master 主分支上运行 git merge 命令，将 login 分支的代码合班到 master 主分支</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git merge login</font></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">删除分支</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">切换到主分支然后执行删除</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git branch -D login  #删除login分支</font></div></div><div>
</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">遇到冲突时的分支合并</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [54].png)发生冲突代码</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="font-size: 18.6667px; font-weight: bold;">找到发生冲突的代码进行处理 ，然后提交</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [55].png)</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">打开这些包含冲突的文件然后手动解决冲突。</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">将本地分支推送到远程仓库</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># -u 表示把本地分支和远程分支进行关联，只在第一次推送的时候需要带 -u 参数 以后直接用git push就可以推送</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git push -u 远程仓库的别名 本地分支名称:远程分支名称</font></div><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 实际案例</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git push -u origin payment:pay</font></div><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 如果希望远程分支的名称和本地分支名称保持一致，可以对命令进行简化</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git push -u origin payment</font></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: Monaco; font-weight: bold;">查看远程仓库所有的分列表</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font face="Gadugi" style="font-size: 14pt;">git remote show 远程仓库名称</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="font-size: 18.6667px; font-weight: bold;">跟踪分支（在远程仓库把分支拉到本地）</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 示例</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git checkout pay</font></div><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 从远程仓库中，把对应的远程分支下载到本地仓库，并把下载的本地分支进行重命名</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git checkout -b 本地分支名称 远程仓库名称/远程分支名称</font></div><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 示例</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git checkout -b payment origin/pay</font></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">拉取远程分支的最新代码</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font color="#DE5700" style="font-size: 14pt;"># 从远程仓库，拉取当前分支最新的代码，保持当前分支的代码和远程分支代码一致</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git pull</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">删除远程分支</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><font color="#DE5700"># 删除远程仓库中，制定名称的远程分支</font></font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git push 远程仓库名称 --delete 远程分支名称</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><font color="#DE5700"># 示例</font></font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">git push origin --delete pay</font></div></div><div>
</div>

# <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 2; position: relative; cursor: text; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); white-space: pre-wrap; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 24pt; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 1.2;">总结</span></span>

- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">能够掌握</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">Git</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">中基本命令的使用</span></div>

- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">git init 初始化</span></div>
- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">git add . 添加修改的文件到暂存仓库</span></div>
- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">git commit –m &quot;提交消息&quot; 提交到本地仓库</span></div>
- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">git status</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">和</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">git status -s 查看文件的状态</span></div>*   <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">能够使用</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">Github</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">创建和维护远程仓库</span></div>

- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">能够配置</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">Github</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">的</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">SSH</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">访问</span></div>
- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">能够将本地仓库上传到</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">Github</span></div>*   <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">能够掌握</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.9em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">Git</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">分支的基本使用</span></div><div>

<span><div>流式布局 ：百分比布局 经典的自适应布局</div><div>

<a name="941"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_node_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div><div><span style="font-weight: bold;">在当前目录打开cmd   输入     node 要运行的文件   来运行</span></div><div>
</div><div><span style="font-weight: bold;">cmd快捷指令</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [56].png)</div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">1</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-style: italic; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">c</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">onst</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;"> </span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">fs</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;"> </span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">=</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;"> </span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">require</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">'fs'</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">); 导入fs模块 文件模块</span></font></div>

- <div><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial;">fs.readFile(文件的路径,[编码格式],回调函数(err(失败),dataStr(成功))) 读取指定的文件中的内容,无法动态创建文件夹</span></span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial;">fs.writeFile(路径,写入的内容,[格式],回调函数)  在指定的文件中写入内容</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">
  </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">路径拼接错误的问题,解决方法,使用绝对路径(完整的路径); </span> <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);font-size: 14pt;-evernote-highlight:true;">原因 使用相对路径 是以 终端定位的位置 去拼接的</span></div><div><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);font-size: 14pt;-evernote-highlight:true;">__dirname 表示当前文件所处的目录</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">
  </span></font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">2.</span></font><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">const</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;"> path = require('path');</span><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">导入path 路径模块 处理路径</span></span></font></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Consolas;">path.join(</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Consolas;"> __dirname, ''</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Consolas;">)  拼接多个路径片段 拼接成一个完整的路径  ../会抵消路径</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">path.basename('路径',[</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">扩展名</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">])  拿到</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">文件的文件名,不希望拿到扩展名可以传两个参数</span></div>
- <div><span style="font-size: 16px;">path.extname('路</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">径最</span><span style="font-size: 16px;">径') 拿到扩展名</span></div><div><span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
  </span></div></div><div>
  </div></span>
  </div>

<div>
<span><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;"><span style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">服务器本质是提供服务的软件</span></span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold;">域名服务器 提供ip地址和域名之间的转换服务的服务器(存的是各种对应关系)</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span>    </span>输入域名-----&gt;域名服务器找到对应的ip----&gt;服务器</font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span>    </span>静态资源 : html css js等一些</font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span>    </span>动态资源 : 用数据库动态生成的一些资源</font></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">在服务器运行的html中 ./ 表示当前访问的文件的同级目录,</span> <span style="font-size: 15pt;">/ 表示服务器根目录</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">
</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">

</span></span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); line-height: 27px;">);</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242);">})</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); line-height: 27px;">// 4启动服务器</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); line-height: 27px;">console</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); line-height: 27px;">'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); line-height: 27px;">);</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); line-height: 27px;">})</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;white-space: pre;background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">
</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">require(文件地址)导入自定义模块</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">require(第三方模块名) 导入第三方模块</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">require引入模块会执行模块中的代码</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">
</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">只有</span> <span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">module</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">exports 可以导出 暴露出去</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">exports ===</span> <span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">module</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 27px;">exports</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="white-space: pre; font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">exports不能重新赋值</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">![](前端_files/Image [57].png)</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">修改npm的下载源为淘宝镜像</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="min-height: 20pt; font-size: 15pt; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">npm config set registry [https://registry.npm.taobao.org](https://registry.npm.taobao.org/)</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">

border: 1px solid;"><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;"> npm i</span></div></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align: middle; width: 279px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">package.json 三个不可缺少的属性</span></font></div></td><td style="width: 686px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;"> name 项目名</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;"> main 包的主入口 默认是 index.js</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;"> description  描述</span></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">![](前端_files/Image [58].png)</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 16pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">模块查找机制</span></font><span style="font-weight: bold;">    </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">模块会优先从缓存中加载</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">  </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">  </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">内置模块</span></div><div>      <span style="font-size: 12pt;">  优先级最高 如果node_modules中有与内置模块重名的 优先加载内置模块</span></div><div>  <span style="font-size: 12pt;"> </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;"> </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">自定义模块</span></div><div>      <span style="font-size: 12pt;">  按填入的路径引入，如果省略后缀名 会依次</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            .js</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            .json</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            .node</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            如果以上后缀名都木有 就报错</span></div><div> <span style="font-size: 12pt;"> </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;"> </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;"> 第三方模块</span></div><div>        <span style="font-size: 11pt;">查找规则</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;">            先在当前项目目录中的node_modules中查找</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;">            如果没有 就翻到上一次再次查找node_modules</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 11pt;">            一直向上翻到盘符目录下 找不到 就报错</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">   </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">引用包名为目录</span></div><div>       <span style="font-size: 12pt;"> require('/router')     </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">router是一个目录（文件夹）</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            会默认读取目录中的package.json</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                读取package.json中的main指定的入口文件</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            如果目录中没有package.json 则默认查找index.js文件 引入</span></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">Express插件 npm i express安装</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">req</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">, </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">res</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">) </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(102, 217, 239); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">=&gt;</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> {</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    // req.query 默认是一个空对象,拿到的是查询字符串 'user?name=zs&amp;age=18'</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    // req.params 动态匹配到的url参数,默认是一个空对象</span> <span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'user/:id/:name'</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">res</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">send</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">({ </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">name</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">: </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'张三'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">, </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">age</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">: </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(174, 129, 255); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">18</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> })</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">})</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">app</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'/user'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">, (</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">req</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">, </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">res</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">) </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(102, 217, 239); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">=&gt;</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> {</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">res</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">send</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'请求成功'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">)</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">})</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">//设置静态资源目录 第一个参数是添加访问前缀,不填就指定的目录下的资源就在网站的根目录</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(50, 135, 18); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">/</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(65, 173, 28); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">/</span><span style="min-height: 13pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(65, 173, 28); font-family: ΢���ź�; line-height: 27px;">传入第一个参数name之后 访问静态资源目录中的文件时 就必须携带name</span></span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">app</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">use</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">('/name',</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">express</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">static</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'./clock'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">))</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(130, 224, 170); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">//3 启动服务器</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">app</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">listen</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(174, 129, 255); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">80</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">, () </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(102, 217, 239); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">=&gt;</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> {</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">console</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(102, 217, 239); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">log</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'</span>[http://127.0.0.1](http://127.0.0.1/)<span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">);</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">})</span></div><div>
</div><div>
</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">路由</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">  </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">服务端中的路由就是 请求地址与处理函数的 对应关系</span></div>

- <div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"> </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">路由的组成部分</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
  </span></div><div>         ![](前端_files/Image [59].png)</div><div>
  </div><div>
  </div></div><div>
  </div></span>
  </div>

---

<a name="970"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_node_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">express 的路由模块(步骤)</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    1.const express=require('express');</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    2.const router=express.Router();  //创建路由模块</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    3.router.get(url,handler);  //挂载路由</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    4.module.exports=router</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">; //导出路由</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="font-size: 18.6667px; font-weight: bold;">引入路由模块</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    1.const router=require(路由模块的路径) //引入路由模块</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">     2.app.use(router)  //挂载到全局中间件</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">给路由模块添加前缀</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;">    app.use(前缀,router)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">中间件</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [60].png) </div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    const mw = function (req,res,next){next()};</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    调用  next()  把流转关系转交给下一个中间件或路由</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">类别</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    1.全局生效的中间件  app.use(mw)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    2.局部生效的中间件  </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">app.get( url,中间件，handler )</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">分类 </span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    1.内置中间件   get put post delete</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        express.static    挂载静态资源</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        express.json    转换json格式的数据</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        express.urlencoded   转换</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">urlencoded 的数据   可以用req.body 拿到</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;">    2.第三方中间件  </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    3.应用级别中间件   </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">app.use（xxxx）</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    4.路由级别中间件   </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">router.use(xxxxx)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;">    5.错误级别中间件   </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">写在路由规则之后 用于捕捉错误</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">中间件的注意点</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    1.  一定要在路由之前注册中间件( 错误处理级别除外 )</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    2.  客户端发送过来的请求，可以连续调用多个中间件进行处理</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    3.  执行完中间件的业务代码之后，不要忘记调用 `next()` 函数</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    4.  为了防止代码逻辑混乱，调用 `next()` 函数后不要再写额外的代码</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    5.  连续调用多个中间件时，多个中间件之间，共享 `req` 和 `res` 对象</span></div><div>
</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">cors   解决浏览器的跨域问题</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    使用方式:</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        1.下载安装第三方的中间件cors; npm i cors</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        2.const cors=require('cors');</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        3.app.use(cors())  要写在路由之前</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    两个请求的概念</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        简单请求 预检请求</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16pt;">jsonp</span></div><div><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">    如果项目中已经配置了</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 0.9em; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">CORS</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">跨域资源共享，为了防止冲突，必须在配置</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 0.9em; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">CORS</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">中间件之前声明</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 0.9em; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">JSONP</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">的接口</span></div><div><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">    否则</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 0.9em; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">JSONP</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">接口会被处理成开启了</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 0.9em; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244); border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: var(--monospace); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">CORS</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; <span><div><span style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 16pt;">sql语句</font></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">增: insert into 表名 set 值 values</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">删: delete from 表名 where xxx  注意！！如果不加where会有可能删除所有的内容</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">改: </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">update 表名 set 属性名</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">查: </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">select * from 表名 , </span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">* 代表所有</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 12pt;">其他语法</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    and  同时满足</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    or   或者</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    where  </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    count(*)  获取总数量</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    as 重命名</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    order by 属性 desc/asc   升序/降序</span></div><div>

</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-clock</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>防止页面加载页面闪烁问题</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;">v-txet</td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>没有闪动问题,用于将数据填充到标签中</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-html</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>用于将html片段填充到标签中   可能有安全隐患</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-pre</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>显示原始信息跳过编译过程</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-once</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>只执行一次的插值 , 当数据改变时,内容不会持续更新</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-model</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>限制在input select textarea  components 中 使用 </div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-on</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>用来绑定事件  v-on:click='fn'    @click='fn()'</div><div>
</div><div>参数的传递</div><div>1,@click='fn'  默认传的是$event 事件对象</div><div>2,@click='fn(a,b,$event)'  如果传别的参数的话 事件对象必须手动传 用 $event</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>事件修饰符</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>&lt;!-- 阻止单击事件继续传播 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;a v-on:click.stop=&quot;doThis&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div><div>
</div><div>&lt;!-- 提交事件不再重载页面 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;form v-on:submit.prevent=&quot;onSubmit&quot;&gt;&lt;/form&gt;</div><div>
</div><div>&lt;!-- 修饰符可以串联   即阻止冒泡也阻止默认事件 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;a v-on:click.stop.prevent=&quot;doThat&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div><div>
</div><div>&lt;!-- 只当在 event.target 是当前元素自身时触发处理函数 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;!-- 即事件不是从内部元素触发的 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;div v-on:click.self=&quot;doThat&quot;&gt;...&lt;/div&gt;</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-bind</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>&lt;!-- 绑定一个属性 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;img v-bind:src=&quot;imageSrc&quot;&gt;</div><div>
</div><div>&lt;!-- 缩写 --&gt;</div><div>&lt;img :src=&quot;imageSrc&quot;&gt;</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-if</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>多个元素通过条件判断 展示或隐藏某个元素,或多个元素</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-show</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-show='false'   让元素隐藏 本质是设置display设置为none</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>v-for</div></td><td style="width: 496px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div><span style="letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">用于循环的数组里面的值可以是对象，也可以是普通元素</span></span>  </div><div>&lt;li v-for=&quot;(item,index) in items&quot;&gt; {{ item.message }} &lt;/li&gt;</div><div>
</div><div>key的作用 高效的更新 虚拟DOM</div><div>&lt;li v-for=&quot;item in items&quot; :key=&quot;item.id&quot;&gt;...&lt;/li&gt;</div><div>
</div><div>可以遍历对象,可以和v-if一起使用</div><div>&lt;div v-if='v==13' v-for='(v,k,i) in obj'&gt;{{v + '---' + k + '---' + i}}&lt;/div&gt;</div></td><td style="width: 427px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>
</div></td></tr><tr><td style="width: 130px; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid;"><div>

</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="font-size: 18.6667px; font-weight: bold;">侦听器: </span></span><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">watch: {}</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">   </span> <span style="font-size: 14pt;">用于监听数据变化</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">可以监听比如 数组长度 或者 路由地址 以及 data vuex的state 计算属性 等等</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); line-height: 27px;">: </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(102, 217, 239); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">function</span><span style="font-size: 20px; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">val</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">) {</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(250, 122, 0); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">// val就是 被监听数据的 新值</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">                    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">console</span><span style="font-size: 20px; </span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">过滤器:</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">    <span style="font-size: 18.6667px; font-weight: bold;">全局过滤器</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">Vue.filter( ‘过滤器名’,function(value){  } )</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">         value是固定的形参 表示要被过滤的值</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        必须要return一个结果</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">    组件过滤器</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    let vm = new Vue({</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">       filters:{</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        过滤器名:function(value){ return }</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        }</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    })</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">![](前端_files/Image [64].png) </span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;
