<a name="988"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_vue_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div>![](前端_files/Image [65].png) </div><div><font style="font-size: 18pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 18pt;"><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">组件的创建</span></font></div><div><font style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">全局组件:</span></font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">Vue.component('组件的名称',配置的对象</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    { data:function() {</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    return {这里面放数据},</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">   },</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    template:``</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">}</font><font style="font-size: 14pt;">)</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">   data是一个函数,并且要把数据对象返回出去</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">   template 是模板,可以用模板字符串,也可以定义一个 template标签 通过 id 选择器获取</font></div></div><div>
</div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">局部组件:</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">放在 vm实例里面 components:{ '组件的名字':组件的配置对象 }   属性里面</font></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 16pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">ptops: 接收外面传来的值</span></font></div><div>
</div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">    数组类型----不进行类型的验证</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">    对象类型----进行验证</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">props:{</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">    title：{</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">        type:String,</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">        required:true，</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">        default:'标题'</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">     }</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">}</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">    对title属性进行预验证</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">      type指定 组件接收的类型</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">      required 指定必传</font></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">      default 表示默认值</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;">        通过属性的方式传递  </span><span style="font-size: 16pt;">&lt;son</span> <span style="font-size: 16pt;">:tiele='msg'</span><span style="font-size: 16pt;">&gt;&lt;/son&gt;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;">        单项数据流: 在子组件不能修改父组件的数据;</span></div><div>
</div><div>
</div><div>
</div><div>
</div></span>
</div>

<a name="1004"/>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_vue_</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<span><div><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">组件中的传值</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">子组件向父组件传值:</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    1.在子组件的声明周期函数上:</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">  </span> <span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(77, 206, 29); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> </span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;-evernote-highlight:true;">    this.$emit() 发布自定义事件</span></span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">            mounted</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">() {</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">                </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">this</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">$emit</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'msg'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">, </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">this</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.sonmsg)</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">            }</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">       </span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(150, 238, 125); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">2.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(150, 238, 125); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">在父组件模板中:</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    &lt;</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(249, 38, 114); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">div</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">id</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">=</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">&quot;app&quot;</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">&gt;</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">        &lt;</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(249, 38, 114); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">son</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">@msg</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">=</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(230, 219, 116); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">'handle'</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">&gt;&lt;/</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(249, 38, 114); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">son</span><span style="font-size: 20px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"><font color="#F8F8F2">&gt;</font> <font color="#328712">/**/**</font></span><span style="font-size: 20px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">**<font style="color: rgb(50, 135, 18);">绑定在组件的事件都是自定义事件</font>**</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    &lt;/</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(249, 38, 114); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">div</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">&gt;</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">
</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(150, 238, 125); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">3.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(150, 238, 125); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">在父组</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(150, 238, 125); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">件的配置对象的方法里:</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">    </span><span style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px;"><span style="font-size: 20px; background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;"> methods: {</span></span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">          </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">handle</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">val</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">) {</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">            </span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">console</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">.</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(166, 226, 46); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">log</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">(</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(253, 151, 31); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-style: italic; line-height: 27px;">val</span><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">);</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">                }</span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; line-height: 27px;">      }</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">兄弟组件之间的传值</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在a事件中 在事件中心发布 b事件的 自定义事件</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在b事件中 在事件中心发布 a事件的 自定义事件</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在事件a中  监听事件中心的 a的事件</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在事件b中  监听事件中心的 b的事件</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">扩展的内容</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">        $parent    </font><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑;">可以在子组件中拿到父组件的实例 , 可以访问父组件的数据</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑;">
</span></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">        $children   </font><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑;">访问子组件的实例 , 是一个数组</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑;">
</span></div><div><font face="微软雅黑" style="font-size: 14pt;">        ref=&quot;自定名字&quot;  </font><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑;">在父组件模板里 给元素标签 或者 组件的标签中定义ref属性</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑;">            通过 $refs.自定义的名字.xxx  得到绑定的属性实例</span></div></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">组件的插槽</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">普通插槽</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        直接在父组件模板中的  子组件标签中间放内容</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在子组件的 模板中用 &lt;slot&gt; &lt;/slot&gt; 标签接收</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">具名插槽</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        1在子组件的模板中给 slot 标签添加name属性</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        2在父组件中 的子组件模板中 使用 &lt;template</span> <span style="font-size: 14pt;">slot='对应的name值' </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">&gt;&lt;/template&gt; 包裹</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        3并且添加 slot='对应的name值'  属性  </span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">  template 里面可以写标签</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">作用域插槽</span> <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">父组件操作子组件上的数据</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在子组件中的 solt标签上  绑定一个自定义的属性</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">template:`</font><span style="font-size: 14pt;">&lt;solt  :自定义的属性='item' &gt;&lt;/slot&gt;`</span></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        在父组件模板的子组件标签中 使用 slot-scope 拿到这个属性的值</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Monaco;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;">&lt;son&gt;</font></span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">        &lt;template slot-scope='自定义名'&gt;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">            &lt;div&gt;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">                {{自定义名.自定义属性.XXX}}</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">            &lt;/div&gt;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">        &lt;/template&gt;</font></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Monaco;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;">&lt;/son&gt;</font></span></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">![](前端_files/Image [66].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"> ![](前端_files/Image [67].png)</span></div></span>

<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td>**标签：**</td><td>_vue_</td></tr>

<div>
<span><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">js执行机制:</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">![](前端_files/Image [68].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">![](前端_files/Image [69].png)</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">promise</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    解决回调地狱问题</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    new promise(function(resolve,reject){})</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        resolve() 回调,成功执行</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        reject()回调, 失败后执行</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">实例的方法</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">     </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">   .then()</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            得到 promise函数 正确的结果,两个参数,</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                resolve的函数体</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                    接收promise实例里面的 resolve的实参</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                reiect的函数体</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                    接收 promise实例里面的 reject的实参</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                只有一个参数就是执行resolve的函数体</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">      </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">  .catch()</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            得到异常的结果</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                如果 .then 没有传失败的回调,当异步执行失败后,会调用</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                如果 .then传了失败的回调,可以捕捉.then里面的 成功的回调报错,或失败的回调报错</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">.finally()</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            无论成功还是失败都会运行</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">静态的方法</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        .all([a,b,c].then())</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            发送并且处理多个异步任务</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        .rece([a,b,c].then())</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            发送多个异步任务,只处理最快结果的异步任务</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">Fetch</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">   fetch('http://localhost:3000/fdata').then(function(data){</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">       // text()方法属于fetchAPI的一部分，它返回一个Promise实例对象，用于获取后台返回的数据</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">       return data.text();</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">     }).then(function(data){</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">        // 在这个then里面我们能拿到最终的数据</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">        console.log(data);</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">     })</font></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    内置的api 基于promise 封装的发送请求的api</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        发送的不是ajax请求 是fetch请求</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    fetch('url',config)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        url 请求的地址</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        config 请求的参数对象{}</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            method 请求额类型</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            body 请求体</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            headers  设置请求头</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                如果发送其他的形式要设置'Content-type':'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'  或者 'Content-Type': </span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">axios</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">![](前端_files/Image [70].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">![](前端_files/Image [71].png) </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">   </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">全局配置</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">     axios.defaults.timout=3000    超时时间</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">     axios.defaults.beseURl='</span><a href="http://xxx/" style="font-size: 12pt;">http://XXX</a><span style="font-size: 12pt;">' 配置基准的url</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">     </span>[axios.defaults.headers.common](http://axios.defaults.headers.common/)<span style="font-size: 12pt;">['my token']='XX' 设置公共的请求头</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">     axios.defaults.headers.post['Content-Type'] = 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded';   配置公共的 post 的 Content-Type</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">   </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;"> 拦截器</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">       </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;"> 拦截请求</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            axios.interceptors.request.use(function(config){})</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                一定要把config  return出去</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">      </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">  拦截响应</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">            axios.interceptors.response.use(function(res){})</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                res就是响应回来的对象</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">                    可以修改完 return出去</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">async/await</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    async 修饰的函数 会默认隐式的返回一个Promise对象</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: bold;">await 的使用注意点</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        1 await只能写在 async修饰的函数内</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        2 await 只能修饰 Promise 对象</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        3 await 相当于把它修饰的Promise对象中 resolve的实参扣了出来 返回给变量</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">    async/await 让异步代码看起来、表现起来更像同步代码</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">        await修饰的异步操作不执行完 主线就不会继续往下执行</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 12pt;">

</div>

<div>
<span><div><div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">路由的概念</span></font></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    路由就是对应关系</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">前端路由</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        事件对应的页面响应</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        根据不同的事件来显示不同的页面内容，即事件与事件处理函数之间的对应关系</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">    SPA  </span></font><span style="font-size: 14pt;">single page appliaction</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        单页面应用</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        整个网站只有一个页面，内容的变化通过Ajax局部更新实现、同时支持浏览器地址栏的前进和后退操作</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">        基于URL地址的hash（hash的变化会导致浏览器记录访问历史的变化、但是hash的变化不会触发新的URL请求）</span></div>

### <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 2; position: relative; cursor: text; white-space: pre-wrap; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: 1.43;">Vue Router</span></span> <span style="font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: 1.43;">Vue.js 官方提供的路由管理器</span>

</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">动态路由匹配</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Monaco;">&lt;router-link to=&quot;user/123&quot;&gt;&lt;/</span><font style="font-size: 14pt;">router-link</font><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Monaco;">&gt;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Monaco;">...</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">var User = { template:&quot;&lt;div&gt;用户：{{$route.params.id}}&lt;/div&gt;&quot;}   //被动接收</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">var myRouter = new VueRouter({</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">//routes是路由规则数组</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">routes: [</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    //通过/:参数名  的形式传递参数 </font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    { path: &quot;/user/:id&quot;, component: User },</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">]</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">})</font></div></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">通过props来接收参数 主动接收</span></span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**    { path: &quot;/user/:id&quot;, component: User, <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">props:true</span> } <font color="#4F009A">//设置props为 true</font>**</font></div></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**<span style="font-size: 14pt;">    </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑; color: rgb(65, 0, 125);">//如果props设置为对象，则传递的是对象中的数据给组件</span>**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**<span style="font-size: 14pt;">    { path: &quot;/user/:id&quot;, component: User, props:{username:&quot;jack&quot;,pwd:123} }</span>**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**
**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**<span style="font-size: 14pt;">  </span> <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;"> </span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 微软雅黑; color: rgb(28, 51, 135);">//如果想要获取传递的参数值还想要获取传递的对象数据，那么props应该设置为 函数形式</span>**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**    <span style="font-size: 14pt;">{ path: &quot;/user/:id&quot;, component: User, props:(route)=&gt;(</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">return {username:&quot;jack&quot;,pwd:123,id:route.params.id}</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">)</span><span style="font-size: 14pt;">}</span>**</font></div></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">在组件中添加props接收</span></font></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**    var User = {**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**    props:[&quot;id&quot;,&quot;username&quot;,&quot;pwd&quot;],**</font></div><div>**<font style="font-size: 14pt;">    template:&quot;&lt;div&gt;用户：</font><font style="font-size: 14pt;">{{id}} -&gt; {{username}}---{{pwd}}</font><font style="font-size: 14pt;">&lt;/div&gt;&quot;</font>**</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**    }**</font></div></div><div style="line-height: 27px; white-space: pre;"></div>

#### <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 2; font-size: 1.25em; position: relative; cursor: text; white-space: pre-wrap; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 1.4;">命名路由：给路由取别名</span>

<div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 8px; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(251, 250, 248); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);-en-codeblock:true;"><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">var myRouter = new VueRouter({</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    //routes是路由规则数组</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    routes: [</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">        **//通过name属性为路由添加一个别名**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">        { path: &quot;/user/:id&quot;, component: User, <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">name:&quot;user&quot;</span>},</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    ]</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">})</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**//添加了别名之后，可以使用别名进行跳转**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">&lt;router-link <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">:to</span>=&quot;{ <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">name:'user'</span> , params: {id:123} }&quot;&gt;User&lt;/router-link&gt;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">**//还可以编程式导航**</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">myRouter.push( { name:'user' , params: {id:123} } )</font></div></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">页面导航的两种方式：</span></span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: 27px;">A.声明式导航：通过点击链接的方式实现的导航</span></font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: 27px;">B.编程式导航：调用js的api方法实现导航</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0.8em 0px; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">    this.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: nowrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: normal; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline-block; zoom: 0.9; word-wrap: normal; direction: ltr; max-width: none; max-height: none; min-width: 0px; min-height: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: normal;">$</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">router.push(&quot;/login&quot;);</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: 27px;">    this.$</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; font-size: 14pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; line-height: 27px;">router.go( -1 );</span></font></div><div style="white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">路由导航守卫</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 21.3333px;">**全局**</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">router.beforEach((to,form,next)=&gt;{})</span></div><div>![](前端_files/Image [72].png)</div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">只有 next() 才会放行 </span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">所有的页面跳转都会进入</span>
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 21.3333px; font-weight: bold;">局部</span>
</div><div style="white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">beforRouteEnter(to,from,next)=&gt;{} 可以判断在哪个路由跳转进来 在mounted后执行</span>
</div><div style="white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">beforRouteLeave(to,from,next)=&gt;{} 路由跳转前执行, 可以判断去哪个页面 可以选择 缓存或者不缓存</span>
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">配合 路由额 meta:{keepLeave: true}</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 16pt;">
</font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 16pt;">**路由缓存**</font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 16pt;">**
**</font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 16pt;">**方法一:**</font></div><div style="white-space: pre;"></div><div style="white-space: pre;"></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">{ path: &quot;/user/:id&quot;, component: User, meta:{</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">keepAlive:true</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">}</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">}</span> <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(79, 0, 154);">//设置</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">keepAlive</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(79, 0, 154);">为 true</span>
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(79, 0, 154);">
</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">方法二:</span>
</div><div style="background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45); color: rgb(204, 204, 204); font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; </font></div><div style="background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45); color: rgb(204, 204, 204); font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-variant-caps: normal; <div>
<span><div>**<font style="font-size: 14pt;">默认导出</font>**</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">export default {</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    成员A,</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    成员B,</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    .......</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">},如下：</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">let num = 100;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">export default{</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">    num</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">}</font></div><div>**<font style="font-size: 14pt;">默认导入</font>**</div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">import 接收名称 from &quot;模块标识符&quot;，如下：</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">import test from &quot;./test.js&quot;</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">**按需导出**</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">export let num = 998;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">export let myName = &quot;jack&quot;;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">export function fn = function(){ console.log(&quot;fn&quot;) }</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">**按需导入**</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">import { num,fn as printFn ,myName } from &quot;./test.js&quot;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">//同时导入默认导出的成员以及按需导入的成员</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">import test,{ num,fn as printFn ,myName } from &quot;./test.js&quot;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">**
**</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;">**直接导入并执行**</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">import &quot;./test2.js&quot;;</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">**vue单文件组件**</span></div><div><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">1).template组件组成的模板区域</span></div><div><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">2).script组成的业务逻辑区域</span> </div><div><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">3).style样式区域 添加</span> <span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">scoped 属性 表示css只在当前组件中生效</span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">

<span><div><span style="font-size: 21.3333px;"><span style="font-size: 21.3333px; font-weight: bold;"> vue 脚手架  </span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 21.3333px;"><span style="font-size: 21.3333px; font-weight: bold;">1,vue create 项目名字</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 21.3333px;"><span style="font-size: 21.3333px; font-weight: bold;">2,选择方式 选择功能</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [73].png)</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">2,是否使用历史模式的路由</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [74].png)</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;">3,怎样创建配置文件  默认选第一项 单独创建配置文件 </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;">![](前端_files/Image [75].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt;">4,是否保存这个项目</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [76].png)</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt;">
</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt;">
</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">路由导航守卫</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">router.beforEach((to,form,next)=&gt;{})</span></span></div><div><span style="font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [77].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">只有 next() 才会放行 </span></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">所有的页面跳转都会进入</span></font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;">
</font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">组件的名字就是类名</span></font></div><div><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">

</span></font></div><div><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">$nextTick</span> <span style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; line-height: 27px;">在数据更新完,也就是页面被重新渲染之后(Dom更新完) 会立即调用里面的回调函数里的代码</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 20px;"><span style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold;">----适用于刚更新完数据,立即操作dom</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [78].png)  </span></span></div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">Mutation 修改vuex中的数据 <span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165); font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;-evernote-highlight:true;">不能执行异步操作</span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);font-size: 16pt;-evernote-highlight:true;">第一种方式</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18pt;"><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-weight: bold;">![](前端_files/Image [85].png)</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">触发时传参数   Mutation 上的函数只能接受两个参数,第一个参数必须是state</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 18.6667px;background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">        如果有多个参数,可以放在一个对象里面传递</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">![](前端_files/Image [86].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16pt;background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);-evernote-highlight:true;">第二种方式</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">![](前端_files/Image [87].png)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14pt;">

- <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold;">使用下面的代码粘贴到调试工具中运行一下，然后滚动页面，就可以看到是哪个元素产生的滚动了</span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">function findscroller(element) {</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">  element.onscroll = function () {</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">    console.log(element)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">  }</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">  Array.from(element.children).forEach(findscroller)</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">}</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">findscroller(document.body)</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
  </div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">在移动端，视口单位相对于布局视口</span></span></div>

  </div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">.sync 修饰符</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">父组件给子组件传值 的时候 如果子组件要修改父组件的传来的值 可以在父组件 传值时绑定.sync</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">在字组件操作函数中 执行</span></div><div style="white-space: pre;"><span style="letter-spacing: normal;   </div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">正则表达式</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 18px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(77, 77, 77); font-family: &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, &quot;SF Pro Display&quot;, Roboto, Noto, Arial, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">var p=/cat/g;   //字面量声明</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 18px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(77, 77, 77); font-family: &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, &quot;SF Pro Display&quot;, Roboto, Noto, Arial, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">var p=new RegExp('cat','g') //构造函数声明</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 18px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">
  </span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"></div>

### <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 2; font-size: 1.5em; position: relative; cursor: text; white-space: pre-wrap; letter-spacing: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-weight: bold; line-height: 1.43;">关于后端返回数据中的大数字问题     </span>

<div><a href="https://github.com/sidorares/json-bigint" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); cursor: pointer; -webkit-user-drag: none; color: rgb(65, 131, 196); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">json-bigint</a> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(119, 119, 119); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">是一个第三方包，它可以帮我们很好的处理这个问题。</span> <span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(119, 119, 119); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">  npm i json-bigint -S</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(119, 119, 119); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">JSONBig</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(119, 119, 119); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">.stringify()   转成json格式的字符串</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(119, 119, 119); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">JSONBig</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: rgb(119, 119, 119); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;;">.parse()  转成对象格式</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12pt;">
</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 15pt;">// 使用的时候需要把 BigNumber 类型的数据转为字符串来使用</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">console.log(JSONBig.parse(jsonStr).art_id.</span><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 250, 165);font-size: 15pt;-evernote-highlight:true;">toString()</span><span style="font-size: 15pt;">) // 1245953273786007552</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">// 把 JavaScript 对象 转为 JSON 格式的字符串</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">console.log(JSONBig.stringify(JSONBig.parse(jsonStr)))</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">[https://github.com/sindresorhus/github-markdown-css](https://github.com/sindresorhus/github-markdown-css)</span> [github-markdown-css](https://github.com/sindresorhus/github-markdown-css)<span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 4; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: pre-wrap; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">样式文件</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="white-space: pre;"><font style="font-size: 16pt;"><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-weight: bold;">v-model 给组件传值</span></font></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">在子组件props中 默认通过 value 接收</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">默认事件名称为 input</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">修改默认的事件名称 默认的 props 名称</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 15pt;">![](前端_files/Image [96].png)</span></div><div style="font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;">
</div><div style="background-color: rgb(39, 40, 34); font-size: 20px; white-space: pre;"><span style="font-size: 20px; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; 1.  <div style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">如果是基于服务端的裁切，则使用：</span>[getData](https://github.com/fengyuanchen/cropperjs#getdatarounded) <span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: 4; white-space: pre-wrap; position: relative; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Clear Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal;">方法，该方法得到裁切的区域参数</span></div>
